You will have the opportunity to own a specific vertical within one of the product surface areas below based on your skillset, interest, and Ramp\u2019s business needs. You will define and evolve our end-to-end product vision, strategy, and execution to meet ambitious company goals.\n\nWe\u2019re looking for someone who can partner and collaborate across various internal teams, has a deep understanding of our customers and technology, and deliver financial products to streamline complex business flows via a fantastic user experience.\n\n\n\n*Please note that this Product Management role will require you to be comfortable with working in-person at our NYC HQ (located near Madison Square Park) at least 2 days/week*\n\n\n\n\nWHAT YOU\u2019LL DO\n\n - Our mission is to help build healthier businesses, and it\u2019s working: over 15,000 businesses on Ramp to save an average 5% and close their books 8x faster.\u00a0\n\n\n\nFounded in 2019, Ramp powers the fastest-growing corporate card and bill payment platform in America, and enables tens of billions of dollars in purchases each year.\u00a0\n\n\n\nRamp's investors include Founders Fund, Stripe, Citi, Goldman Sachs, Coatue Management, D1 Capital Partners, Redpoint Ventures, General Catalyst, and Thrive Capital, as well as over 100 angel investors who were founders or executives of leading companies. The Ramp team comprises talented leaders from leading financial services and fintech companies\u2014Stripe, Affirm, Goldman Sachs, American Express, Mastercard, Visa, Capital One\u2014as well as technology companies such as Meta, Uber, Netflix, Twitter, Dropbox, and Instacart. In 2023, Ramp was named Fast Company\u2019s #1 Most Innovative Company in North America, LinkedIn\u2019s #1 Top Startup in the U.S., a CNBC Disruptor, and a TIME100 Most Influential Company.\n\n\n\nAbout the Role\u00a0\n\n\n\nYou will be a front-line manager to a group of 5-8 Account Managers, who each manage a book of ~200 customers in Ramp\u2019s critical SMB portfolio. You will be responsible for 1:1 coaching and mentoring, as well as developing strategy and working closely with leaders across Sales, Marketing, Operations, Risk, Product, and the executive team to drive positive outcomes for this segment. As a key member of the sales leadership team, you will have the opportunity to help build and refine Ramp\u2019s account management motion.\n\n\n\nWhat You\u2019ll Do\n\n\n\n - Set and maintain a high-performing culture and morale by managing a group of exceptional 5-8 Account Managers\n\n - Hire and train new Account Managers on Ramp\u2019s product, buyer personas, competition, and tools through various methods (ie. role-plays)\n\n - Develop and execute career development and leadership plans for direct reports; inclusive of but not limited to daily 1:1 mentoring, coaching on sales skills, diving into customer call feedback, and leading enablement sessions\n\n - Engage frequently with customers and build relationships with key contacts / accounts\n\n - Oversee the daily activities and quota performance management of individual Account Managers to ensure key performance metrics are met\n\n - Ensure the SMB AM team exceeds spend activation, product activation, retention, expansion, and customer health goals\n\n - Build Salesforce dashboards to monitor the success of our customers and the performance of the team\n\n - Report on team performance and forecast to senior leadership\n\n - Improve team output and efficiency over time by optimizing systems and processes\n\n - Establish a library of playbook resources for the Account Management team\n\n - Represent the Account Management team cross-functionally with leaders of other departments\n\n\n\nWhat You\u2019ll Need\u00a0\n\n\n\n - Minimum of 2 years of quota-carrying sales or account management experience as an individual contributor, with a proven, consistent track record exceeding goals\n   \n   - Cross and upsell experience is a plus\n\n - Minimum of 4 years of experience building and leading account management teams with a proven track record of exceeding goal\n\n - Prior demonstrated success in fast-paced, results-oriented GTM environments, ideally at SaaS companies\n\n - A passion and excitement for hiring, with a thoughtful approach to team planning and development\n\n - Ability to articulate contractual, technical, and financial value points to customers, including executive leaders\n\n - Strong track record of negotiating, structuring and executing complex sales agreements\n\n - Proficiency in data analytics tools (ie. Salesforce, Looker, and Excel)\n\n - Ability to leverage data to drive decisions, create systems, and identify process improvements to improve efficiency\n\n - Strong collaboration and influencing skills, demonstrated through excellent communication and presentation skills\n\n\n\nNice-to-Haves\u00a0\n\n\n\n - Experience with financial services sales\n\n - Experience at a high-growth startup\n\n - Bachelor\u2019s degree from an accredited university\n\n\n\nCompensation\n\n\n\n - The annual salary/OTE range for the target level for this role is $212,500-$250,000 + target equity + benefits (including medical, dental, vision, and 401(k)\n\n\n\n\nBENEFITS (FOR U.S.-BASED FULL-TIME EMPLOYEES)\n\n - 100% medical, dental & vision insurance coverage for you\n   \n   - Partially covered for your dependents\n   \n   - One Medical annual membership\n\n - 401k (including employer match on contributions made while employed by Ramp)\n\n - Flexible PTO\n\n - Fertility HRA (up to $5,000 per year)\n\n - WFH stipend to support your home office needs\n\n - Wellness stipend\n\n - Parental Leave\n\n - Relocation support\n\n - Pet insurance"

You\u2019ll be partnering with Customer Success &amp; Account Manager teams to identify, prioritize and build financial solutions for existing customers so that Ramp continues to scale with their needs.</p><p style=\"min-height:1.5em\">You will act as the technical and financial subject matter expert for our customers, and design solutions that address the customer\u2019s needs through Ramp and partner integrations. You will partner with Post-Sales teams to drive Product, Design and Engineering teams\u2019 roadmaps to evolve Ramp to better serve our customers at scale and offer increasingly higher value to the customers.</p><p style=\"min-height:1.5em\">You will define the customer\u2019s financial &amp; technical success criteria from onboarding through activation and expansion. You will represent Product, Design and Engineering externally and will operate with deep conviction and understanding of Ramp\u2019s technical capabilities. The role requires technical skills necessary to understand and educate on robust accounting features, and integrate them across all the touchpoints and surface area of a customer.</p><p cost-benefit/ROI analysis, and technical competencies\u00a0</p></li><li><p style=\"min-height:1.5em\">Work directly with onboarding specialists to support more complex technical &amp; accounting implementations of Ramp</p></li><li><p style=\"min-height:1.5em\">Be a subject matter expert across our HRIS and Accounting integration partners, partnering with Sales, Product and partners to advocate for integration development in-line with customer needs\u00a0</p></li><li><p style=\"min-height:1.5em\">Support technical documentation and maintenance of our internal knowledge base for customer use cases and best practices\u00a0</p></li><li><p style=\"min-height:1.5em\">Partner closely with the product team to ensure customer feedback and pain points are heard, reviewed, and
